  <script>
   (function(){
		var removeClass = function(el, className) {
			if (el.classList) {
					el.classList.remove(className);
			} else {
					el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(^|\\b)' + className.split(' ').join('|') + '(\\b|$)', 'gi'), ' ');
			}
		};
		var addClass = function(el, className) {
			if (el.classList) {
					el.classList.add(className);
			} else {
					el.className += ' ' + className;
			}
		};
		if (typeof Object.assign != 'function') {
			// Must be writable: true, enumerable: false, configurable: true
			Object.defineProperty(Object, "assign", {
				value: function assign(target, varArgs) { // .length of function is 2
					'use strict';
					if (target == null) { // TypeError if undefined or null
						throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');
					}
					var to = Object(target);
					for (var index = 1; index < arguments.length; index++) {
						var nextSource = arguments[index];
						if (nextSource != null) { // Skip over if undefined or null
							for (var nextKey in nextSource) {
								// Avoid bugs when hasOwnProperty is shadowed
								if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(nextSource, nextKey)) {
									to[nextKey] = nextSource[nextKey];
								}
							}
						}
					}
					return to;
				},
				writable: true,
				configurable: true
			});
		}
		var myAccountHeader = document.getElementById('myaccount-header');

		var userToken = window.localStorage.getItem('userToken');
		if (userToken !== null) {
			var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
			xhr.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
				if (this.readyState === XMLHttpRequest.DONE && this.status === 200) {
					var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
					var loyaltyStatus = window.sessionStorage.getItem('loyaltyStatus');
					var provider = (Array.isArray(response.identities) && response.identities.length > 0) ? response.identities[0].provider : response.identities.provider;

					// Store the metadata on a session object
					window.sessionStorage.removeItem('loyaltyMetadata'); // Remove it first if exists
					var loyaltyMetadata = Object.assign({}, {
						email: response.email || '',
						firstName: response.given_name || '',
						surname: response.family_name || '',
					}, (response.user_metadata || {}));

					window.sessionStorage.setItem('loyaltyMetadata', JSON.stringify(loyaltyMetadata)); // Set it for later use

					myAccountHeader.innerHTML = response.email + (loyaltyStatus ? ' <strong>(' + loyaltyStatus + ')</strong>' : '');

					window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
					window.dataLayer.push({
						myAccount: {
							provider: provider,
							type: 'Login'
						}
					});

					removeClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedout');
					addClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedin');

				}
			});
			xhr.open("POST", "https://arguscarhire.eu.auth0.com/tokeninfo");
			xhr.setRequestHeader("content-type", "application/json");
			xhr.send(JSON.stringify({id_token: userToken}));
		}
	})();
  </script>

    <script>
     function updateCurrency(c) {
		var currencyCode, newURL;
		var serializeQueryString = function (obj) {
			var parts = [];
			for (var i in obj) {
				if (obj.hasOwnProperty(i)) {
					parts.push(encodeURIComponent(i) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(obj[i]));
				}
			}
			return parts.join("&");
		};
		var unserializeQueryString = function () {
			var match;
			var queryStringRegex = /([^&=]+)=?([^&]*)/g;
			var ret = {};
			var haystack = window.location.search;
			haystack = window.location.search.substring(haystack.indexOf('?') + 1, window.location.search.length);
			while ((match = queryStringRegex.exec(haystack))) {
				ret[decodeURIComponent(match[1])] = decodeURIComponent(match[2]);
			}
			return ret;
		};
		var querystring = unserializeQueryString();
		var newCurrencyCode = c.split('|')[1].toUpperCase();

		if (typeof newCurrencyCode == 'string' && newCurrencyCode.length === 3) {

			cookie.set('ec_country', c, {
				path: '/',
				domain: '.' + window.location.hostname,
				expires: 30
			});

			if (typeof querystring['curr'] !== 'undefined') {
				newCurrencyCode = c.split('|')[1].toUpperCase();
				querystring['curr'] = newCurrencyCode;

				newURL = window.location.href.split('?')[0] + '?' + serializeQueryString(querystring) + window.location.hash;

				window.location.replace(newURL);

			} else {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		}
	}
    </script>

   <script>
    /*
  * CT Module - Grouping Generic functionality
  */
 var CT$ = (function() {
	var exports = {};
	// Filter a list (UL/OL) with LI elements that contain text inside (HTML tags are filtered out)
	// @param options Object - the options object whose parameters are used to setup the filter action:
	//        - inputID String - the ID of the input element used to search
	//        - listID String - the ID of the UL element for the list we want to filter

	/**
		*  Filter a list (UL/OL) with LI elements that contain text inside (HTML tags are filtered out)
		*  @argument Object - the options object whose parameters are used to setup the filter action:
		*  @prop inputID String - the ID of the input element used to search
		*  @prop listID String - the ID of the UL element for the list we want to filter
		*
		*  USAGE:
		*      CT$.filterList({
		*          inputID: 'myInputElementID',
		*          listID: 'myListElementID'
		*      });
		*/
	exports.filterList = function(options) {

		// filter elements by string query, hiding those that don't match
		var filterElementsByQuery = function(list, query) {
			var queryLen = query.length;

			list.map(function(row, index){
				// First show element
				row.el.style.display = '';

				if (row.text.indexOf(query.toLowerCase()) < 0) {
					row.el.style.display = 'none';
				}

				return true;
			});
		};

		// strips leading whitespace and condenses all whitespace
		var normalizeQuery = function (q) {
			return (q.replace(/^\s*/g, '').replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' '));
		};

		// compose a search array composed of element references and search text
		var getListArray = function (listID) {
			var listArray = [];
			var list = document.getElementById(listID).children;
			for(var i = 0, len = list.length; i < len; i++) {
				var el = list[i];
				var text = el.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();
				listArray.push({
					el: el,
					text: text
				});
			}
			return listArray;
		};
		// input event handler
		var onInput = function (event) {
			var specialKeyCodeMap = {
				9: 'tab',
				27: 'esc',
				37: 'left',
				39: 'right',
				13: 'enter',
				38: 'up',
				40: 'down'
			};

			var specialKey = specialKeyCodeMap[event.which || event.keyCode];
			if (!specialKey) {
				var inputEl = event.target;
				var query = normalizeQuery(inputEl.value).toLowerCase();
				filterElementsByQuery(inputEl.listArray, query);
			}
		};

		// Get all LI items from the list
		var listArray = getListArray(options.listID);
		// Get the input element reference
		var inputElement = document.getElementById(options.inputID);
		// Store listArray on input element
		inputElement['listArray'] = listArray;
		// add event listener for key pressed on the input element, hopefully cross-browser
		inputElement.addEventListener('keyup', onInput);
	};

	// On Document Ready wrapper, like jQuery $.(fn)
	exports.ready = function (fn) {
		if (document.readyState != 'loading'){
			fn();
		} else {
			document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', fn);
		}
	};

	exports.fadeIn = function(el) {
		el.style.opacity = 0;
		var last = + new Date();
		var tick = function() {
			el.style.opacity = +el.style.opacity + (new Date() - last) / 400;
			last = + new Date();
			if (+el.style.opacity < 1) {
				(window.requestAnimationFrame && requestAnimationFrame(tick)) || setTimeout(tick, 16);
			}
		};
		tick();
	};

	exports.removeClass = function (el, className) {
		if (el.classList) {
			el.classList.remove(className);
		} else {
			el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(^|\\b)' + className.split(' ').join('|') + '(\\b|$)', 'gi'), ' ');
		}
	};

	exports.addClass = function (el, className) {
		if (el.classList) {
			el.classList.add(className);
		} else {
			el.className += ' ' + className;
		}
	};

	return exports;
}());
   </script>
   <script>
    CT$.ready(function(){

	//prevent default link action. used for currency/lang dropdown links
	var haltLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.haltlink');
	for (var i=0,len=haltLinks.length; i < len; i++) {
		var el = haltLinks[i];
		el.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
	  });
	}

	// Instantiate the currency filter
	CT$.filterList({
		inputID: 'currencyFilter',
		listID: 'currencyList'
	});

	// Instantiate the language filter
	CT$.filterList({
		inputID: 'languageFilter',
		listID: 'languageList'
	});

	// Email subscription functionality
	var emailSubscriptionForm = document.getElementById('emailSubmitForm');
	var emailInput = emailSubscriptionForm.querySelector('#email_subscribe');
	var transSignUpSuccess = document.getElementById('trans-SignUpSuccess');

	emailSubscriptionForm.addEventListener('submit', function(event){
		event.preventDefault();
		event.stopPropagation();

		var url = emailSubscriptionForm.getAttribute('action');
		var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
		request.open('POST', url, true);
		request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8');
		request.onreadystatechange = function () {
			if(request.readyState === XMLHttpRequest.DONE && request.status === 200) {
				emailSubscriptionForm.style.display = 'none';
				transSignUpSuccess.style.opacity = 0;
				transSignUpSuccess.style.display = '';
				CT$.fadeIn(transSignUpSuccess);
			}
		};
		request.send('email_subscribe='+emailInput.value);
	});

	// Scroll to top functionality using standards with polyfill above.
	var scrollToTopLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[name="pageTop"]');
	if (scrollToTopLinks.length > 0) {
		for(var i = 0, len = scrollToTopLinks.length; i < len; i++) {
			scrollToTopLinks[i].addEventListener('click', function(event){
				event.preventDefault();
				event.stopPropagation();

				window.scrollTo(0,0);
			});
		}
	}

});

/*dropdown menu*/
var dropdownMenuCurr = document.getElementById("dropdown-menu-curr");
var dropdownButtonCurr = document.getElementById("dropdown-button-curr");
var dropdownMenuLang = document.getElementById("dropdown-menu-lang");
var dropdownButtonLang = document.getElementById("dropdown-button-lang");

document.onclick = check;
function check(e){
  var target = (e && e.target) || (event && event.srcElement);

  //1. Currency dropdown.
  //check if click in menu area, then check id, then check if its hidden. show/hide if not
  if (!checkParent(target, dropdownMenuCurr)) {
    if (checkParent(target, dropdownButtonCurr)) {
      if (dropdownMenuCurr.classList.contains("invisible")) {
        dropdownMenuCurr.style.left = dropdownButtonCurr.getBoundingClientRect().left + 'px';
        dropdownMenuCurr.classList.remove("invisible");
      } else {dropdownMenuCurr.classList.add("invisible");}
    }
     else {
      //if not clicked on maenu area hide /remain hidden
      dropdownMenuCurr.classList.add("invisible");
    }
  }
  //2. language dropdown.
  if (!checkParent(target, dropdownMenuLang)) {
    if (checkParent(target, dropdownButtonLang)) {
      if (dropdownMenuLang.classList.contains("invisible")) {
        dropdownMenuLang.style.left = dropdownButtonLang.getBoundingClientRect().left + 'px';
        dropdownMenuLang.classList.remove("invisible");
      } else {dropdownMenuLang.classList.add("invisible");}
    }
     else {
      dropdownMenuLang.classList.add("invisible");
    }
  }
}

function checkParent(t, elm) {
  while(t.parentNode) {
    if( t == elm ) {return true;}
    t = t.parentNode;
  }
  return false;
}

//Show hide by div id
function toggle_visibility(id) {
	var e = document.getElementById(id);
	if (e.style.display == 'block')
		e.style.display = 'none';
	else
		e.style.display = 'block';
}

//Slide menu
function openNav() {
	//console.log("open nav");
	document.getElementById("Sidenav").style.width = "100%";
	document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
}
function closeNav() {
	//console.log("close nav");
	document.getElementById("Sidenav").style.width = "0";
	document.body.style.overflow = "initial";
}
function openInnerNav(id) {
	document.getElementById(id).style.width = "100%";
}
function closeInnerNav(id) {
	document.getElementById(id).style.width = "0";
}

//Cookie confirmation
if (document.getElementById('js-cookie-disclaimer') !=null){
	var footerCookieDisclaimer = document.getElementById('js-cookie-disclaimer')
	if (cookie.get('cookieDisclaimer')) {
	}
	else{
		footerCookieDisclaimer.classList.remove("dn")
	}
	function acceptDisclaimer() {
		footerCookieDisclaimer.classList.add("dn")
		cookie.set({
			cookieDisclaimer: 'accepted'
		}, {
				path:'/',
				expires: 30
		});
	}
}

					'Damage Refund Insurance': data.vehicleData.amount.insurancePrice,
					'Price Total': data.vehicleData.amount.totalPrice
				};
				window.dataLayer.push(dataLayerItem);
			}catch(err){} }
		},
		confirmation: function (event, status, data, api) {
			if ( status == 'success' ) { try {
				var dataLayerItem = {
					'event': 'step6',
					'Car hire fee': data.vehicleData.amount.price,
					'reservationNumber': data.reservationData.id,
					'totalIncInsurance': data.vehicleData.amount.totalPrice
				};
				window.dataLayer.push(dataLayerItem);

									var parentToAppend = document.querySelector('.ct-body-content');
					if (parentToAppend) {
						var linkEl = document.createElement('a');
						linkEl.setAttribute('href', '//www.arguscarhire.com/app?_$ja=tsid70348clientID=685000&utm_source=arguscarhire&utm_medium=referrel&utm_campaign=');

						var imgEl = document.createElement('img');
						imgEl.setAttribute('class', 'w-100');
						imgEl.setAttribute('src', 'https://ct-images.imgix.net/ctabe/brands/arguscarhire/app/img/desktop-banner-en.png?cs=strip');
						linkEl.appendChild(imgEl);
						parentToAppend.appendChild(linkEl);
					}
				
			}catch(err){} }
		}
	};
   </script>
   <script defer="" src="//ajaxgeo.cartrawler.com/webapp-abe-latest/app-desktop.js" type="text/javascript">
   </script>
  </main>
  <script>
   (function () {
		var removeClass = function (el, className) {
			if (el.classList) {
				el.classList.remove(className);
			} else {
				el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(^|\\b)' + className.split(' ').join('|') + '(\\b|$)', 'gi'), ' ');
			}
		};
		var addClass = function (el, className) {
			if (el.classList) {
				el.classList.add(className);
			} else {
				el.className += ' ' + className;
			}
		};
		if (typeof Object.assign != 'function') {
			// Must be writable: true, enumerable: false, configurable: true
			Object.defineProperty(Object, "assign", {
				value: function assign(target, varArgs) { // .length of function is 2
					'use strict';
					if (target == null) { // TypeError if undefined or null
						throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');
					}
					var to = Object(target);
					for (var index = 1; index < arguments.length; index++) {
						var nextSource = arguments[index];
						if (nextSource != null) { // Skip over if undefined or null
							for (var nextKey in nextSource) {
								// Avoid bugs when hasOwnProperty is shadowed
								if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(nextSource, nextKey)) {
									to[nextKey] = nextSource[nextKey];
								}
							}
						}
					}
					return to;
				},
				writable: true,
				configurable: true
			});
		}

		var myAccountHeader = document.getElementById('ma--container');
		var myAccountHeaderMobile = document.getElementById('myaccount-header-mobile');
		var menuItemsContainer = document.getElementById('ma--container');

		// Logout Action
		menuItemsContainer.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
			event.stopPropagation();
			event.preventDefault();

			if (event.target.getAttribute('data-action') === 'logout') {
				window.localStorage.removeItem('userToken');
				removeClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedin');
				addClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedout');
				myAccountHeader.innerHTML = 'My Account';
				myAccountHeaderMobile.innerHTML = 'My Account';
			}
			window.location = '/my-account';
		});

		var userToken = window.localStorage.getItem('userToken');

		if (userToken !== null) {
			var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
			xhr.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
				if (this.readyState === XMLHttpRequest.DONE && this.status === 200) {
					var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
					var loyaltyStatus = window.sessionStorage.getItem('loyaltyStatus');
					var provider = (Array.isArray(response.identities) && response.identities.length > 0) ? response.identities[0].provider : response.identities.provider;

					// Store the metadata on a session object
					window.sessionStorage.removeItem('loyaltyMetadata'); // Remove it first if exists
					var loyaltyMetadata = Object.assign({}, {
						email: response.email || '',
						firstName: response.given_name || '',
						surname: response.family_name || '',
					}, (response.user_metadata || {}));

					window.sessionStorage.setItem('loyaltyMetadata', JSON.stringify(loyaltyMetadata)); // Set it for later use

					myAccountHeader.innerHTML = response.email + (loyaltyStatus ? ' (' + loyaltyStatus + ')' : '');
					myAccountHeaderMobile.innerHTML = response.email + (loyaltyStatus ? ' <span class="silver normal">(' + loyaltyStatus + ')' : '</span>');

					window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
					window.dataLayer.push({
						myAccount: {
							provider: provider,
							type: 'Login'
						}
					});
					removeClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedout');
					addClass(menuItemsContainer, 'ma--loggedin');

				}
			});
			xhr.open("POST", "https://arguscarhire.eu.auth0.com/tokeninfo");
			xhr.setRequestHeader("content-type", "application/json");
			xhr.send(JSON.stringify({ id_token: userToken }));
		}
	})();
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
